"the rate of change of the radius r is 5"

The radius of a sphere is increasing at the rate of 0.2m/s
Find the rate of increase of a) the volume, b) the surface area when r = 1.6 ^JunwfDY1

The head of a snowman of radius Rcm loses volume be evaporation at a rate proportional to its surface area. Assuming that the head is spherical, that the volume of a sphere is 4/3πR^3cm^3 and that the surface is 4πR^2cm^2. Write down a differential equation for the rate of change of radius of the snowman's head. ^h8vBXCmJ

A population is growing at a rate which is proportional to the size of the population. Write down a differential equation for the growth of the population ^0fX1cYcJ
